***преуспеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:преуспеть.html>преуспе́ть</a> (13248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uspétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспеть.html>преуспе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">preuspétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преуспевать.html>преуспева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to succeed, to be successful, to prosper</li>
<li>to flourish, to thrive, to prosper</li></ol>

***прецедент.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прецедент.html>прецеде́нт</a> (19967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прецедент.html>прецеде́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">precedént</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прецедент.html>прецеде́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прецедент.html>прецеде́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прецедент.html>прецеде́нтов</a></b>)

***при.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> (89)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*prey</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">for</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">per</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pri</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ locative case or prepositional case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>in the presence of</li>
<li>in the time of</li>
<li>at, by</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pri</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">second-person singular imperative imperfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибавление.html>прибавле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribavlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибавление.html>прибавле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибавление.html>прибавле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибавление.html>прибавле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>increase, raise, rise</li>
<li>addition, augmentation</li>
<li>addendum, supplement, appendix</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">балт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">balt</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Balt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибалт.html>приба́лт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribált</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибалт.html>приба́лта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибалт.html>приба́лты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибалт.html>приба́лтов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приба́лтка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> citizen/dweller of one of the Baltic states (usually of Estonia, Latvia or Lithuania)</li></ol>

***прибегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибегать.html>прибега́ть</a> (5755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегать.html>прибега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегнуть.html>прибе́гнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибежать.html>прибежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to resort, to have recourse, to fall back <i>(upon)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегать.html>прибега́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribegátʹ</b> k pómošči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resort to the help; have recourse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегать.html>прибега́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribegátʹ</b> k sile</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resort to force</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегнуть.html>прибе́гнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pribégnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come running
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибежать.html>прибежа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pribežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***прибегнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибегнуть.html>прибе́гнуть</a> (12164)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бегнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">begnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегнуть.html>прибе́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribégnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегать.html>прибега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to resort, to have recourse, to fall back <i>(upon)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегнуть.html>прибе́гнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribégnutʹ</b> k pómošči</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to resort to the help; have recourse</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибегнуть.html>прибе́гнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ле</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribégnutʹ</b> k sile</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to resort to force</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибежать.html>прибежа́вший</a> (4608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибежать.html>прибежа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribežávšij</span>)
</p>

***прибирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибирать.html>прибира́ть</a> (18781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибирать.html>прибира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибрать.html>прибра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put in order, to clean up, to tidy <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибирать.html>прибира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribirátʹ</b> kómnatu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do (clean; tidy up) the room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибирать.html>прибира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribirátʹ</b> postélʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make the bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибирать.html>прибира́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pribirátʹ k rukám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to take in hand; 2) to appropriate, lay one's hands on</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***прибить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибить.html>приби́ть</a> (7991)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибить.html>приби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибивать.html>прибива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to nail down <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to attach with a nail</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to move, to drive somewhere <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the wind or water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to press to the ground <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by an impact or by wind or water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill</li></ol>
